            <div itemprop="articleBody">
             <h2 align="center">
              The Amazing World of Gumball #1 Preview!
             </h2>
             <p>
              <a href="http://www.comicbookcritic.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/AWOG_01_coverA.jpg">
               <img alt="The Amazing World of Gumball #1" border="0" class="colorbox-63705" data-lazy-original="http://www.comicbookcritic.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/AWOG_01_coverA_thumb.jpg" height="376" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAAAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" style="background-image: none; float: none; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; margin: 4px auto; display: block; padding-right: 0px; border: 0px;" title="The Amazing World of Gumball #1" width="512"/>
               <noscript>
                <img alt="The Amazing World of Gumball #1" border="0" class="colorbox-63705" height="376" src="http://www.comicbookcritic.net/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/AWOG_01_coverA_thumb.jpg" style="background-image: none; float: none; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; margin: 4px auto; display: block; padding-right: 0px; border: 0px;" title="The Amazing World of Gumball #1" width="512"/>
               </noscript>
              </a>
             </p>
             <p>
              Heres a preview of
              <em>
               The Amazing World of Gumball #1
              </em>
              by writer
              <strong>
               Frank Gibson
              </strong>
              &amp; artist
              <strong>
               Tyson Hesse
              </strong>
              , courtesy of
              <strong>
               <a class="zem_slink external" href="http://www.boom-studios.com" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.boom-studios.com', 'BOOM! Studios');" rel="homepage" target="_blank" title="Boom! Studios">
                BOOM! Studios
               </a>
              </strong>
               on sale June 25th, 2014.
             </p>
             <p>
             </p>
             <div class="ad-inserter ad-inserter-7" style="text-align:center;margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;margin-top:8px;margin-bottom:8px;">
              <script async="" src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js">
              </script>
              <ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-8092530246159601" data-ad-slot="7781638411" style="display:inline-block;width:300px;height:250px">
              </ins>
              <script>
               (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
              </script>
             </div>
             <h3>
              The Amazing World of Gumball #1
             </h3>
             <p>
              Writer(s):
              <strong>
               Frank Gibson
              </strong>
              <br/>
              Artist(s):
              <strong>
               Tyson Hesse
              </strong>
             </p>
             <p>
              <span id="more-63705">
              </span>
             </p>
             <p align="center">
              <script>
               // 
google_ad_client = "ca-pub-8092530246159601";
/* Medium Rectangle Content - Right Justified */
google_ad_slot = "6873010418";
google_ad_width = 300;
google_ad_height = 250;
// ]]&gt;
              </script>
              <script src="http://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/show_ads.js">
               // &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;// ]]&gt;
              </script>
             </p>
             <p>
              WHY WE LOVE IT: Not only to we get to work with some of our favorite creators on this project, but nothing these days has the mixed-media look of THE AMAZING WORLD OF GUMBALL, and we are the lucky ones who get to bring it to comics!
             </p>
             <p>
              WHY YOULL LOVE IT: Popular webcomic creators
              <strong>
               Frank Gibson
              </strong>
              (TINY KITTEN TEETH) and artist
              <strong>
               Tyson Hesse
              </strong>
              (BOXER HOCKEY) bring the wacky adventures of Gumball and his friends to comics for the first time!
             </p>
             <p>
              WHAT ITS ABOUT: Gumball, Darwin, and all of their friends take on the world of comics! Gumball thinks hes the coolest kid on the block, but his little sister Anais begs to differ, and Darwin just wants to keep them all out of trouble. Theres always another adventure to be had in their mixed-up world!
             </p>
             <p>

   jQuery(document).ready(function(){
var wpfcWpfcAjaxCall = function(polls){
if(polls.length &gt; 0){
poll_id = polls.last().attr('id').match(/\d+/)[0];
poll_nonce = jQuery('#poll_' + poll_id + '_nonce').val();
jQuery.ajax({
type: 'POST',
url: pollsL10n.ajax_url,
dataType : "json",
data : {"action": "wpfc_wppolls_ajax_request", "poll_id": poll_id},
cache: false,
success: function(data){
if(data === true){
poll_result(poll_id);
}else if(data === false){
poll_booth(poll_id);
}
polls.length = polls.length - 1;
setTimeout(function(){
wpfcWpfcAjaxCall(polls);
}, 1000);
}
});
}
};
var polls = jQuery('div[id^=\"polls-\"][id$=\"-loading\"]');
wpfcWpfcAjaxCall(polls);
});
